			#BUDGET SPENDING/COST CODE
			#Number of divisions cost
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = num_divisions
			}
			#Number of Carriers Cost
			set_variable = {
				var = cost_of_carriers
				value = num_ships_with_type@carrier
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_carriers
				value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_carriers
			}
			#Number of Battleship Cost
			set_variable = {
				var = cost_of_battleship
				value = num_ships_with_type@battleship
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_battleship
				value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_battleship
			}
			#Number of Heavy Cruisers Cost
			set_variable = {
				var = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
				value = num_ships_with_type@heavy_cruiser
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
				value = 8
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
			}
			#Number of Light Cruisers Cost
			set_variable = {
				var = cost_of_light_cruiser
				value = num_ships_with_type@light_cruiser

			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_light_cruiser
				value = 5
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_light_cruiser
			}
			#Number of Destroyers Cost

			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_destroyer
				value = 1

			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_destroyer
			}
